                        "content": "<br \/>\nGiliran Ford Terpukul Telak oleh Krisis Eropa<br \/>\n            Ford Motor Company mengumumkan akan segera menghentikan perakitan mobil di pabrik Genk, Belgia, mulai akhir 2014 sebagai dampak dari kondisi ekonomi Eropa yang makin terpuruk. Dengan keputusan ini, produksi model Mondeo dialihkan ke Valencia, Spanyol. Salah satu produsen raksasa mobil Amerika itu memperkirakan pihaknya akan mengalami penurunan sampai 1 miliar dolar AS (Rp 9,6 triliun) pada 2012, terbesar selama 19 tahun terakhir.<br \/>\n            Selain memproduksi Mondeo, pabrik di Belgia itu juga menghasilkan model S-Max dan Galaxy yang juga akan dipindahkan ke Valencia. Sedangkan produksi C-Max dan Gran C-Max yang semula di Valencia, akan digeser ke pabrik Ford lainnya di Saarlouis, Jerman.<br \/>\n            \u201cUsulan restrukturisasi fasilitas manufaktur di Eropa menjadi bagian dari rencana dasar kami untuk memperkuat bisnis Ford di Eropa supaya kembali untung,\u201d komentar Bos Ford Eropa, Stephen Odell. Penggeseran produksi ini berlangsung sukses karena didukung oleh para pekerja.<br \/>\n            Sumber internal Ford mengatakan, Ford juga akan menutup pabriknya di Southampton, Inggris, yang memproduksi sasis untuk Transit, awal tahun depan. Biaya produksi yang besar memaksa Ford harus menghemat, salah satunya dengan memangkas produksi. CEO Ford, Alan Mulally, mengatakan industri otomotif di Eropa harus mengubah ukurannya sesuai kondisi pasar supaya bisa tetap untung.<br \/>\n            Sepanjang 2011, produksi pabrik Southampton hanya 30.000 unit, padahal kapasitas minimum sebuah fasilitas yang sehat adalah 200.000 unit. Brian Johnson, analis dari Barclays di Inggris mengatakan, fasilitas produksi Ford di pabrik itu sebenarnya mencapai 230.000 unit per tahun. \u201cJadi sangat jelas kondisi ini jauh dari semestinya,\u201d jelas Brian.<br \/>\n            Stephen Odell dijadwalkan bertemu dengan serikat pekerja dari seluruh pabrik di Inggris di Dunton, hari ini. \u201cBelum ada topik apa yang akan dibicarakan,\u201d jelas Roger Maddison, pemimpin serikat pekerja Ford yang mewakili 530 pekerja dari pabrik Southampton.<br \/>\n            \u201cKami akan melakukan pengumuman selanjutnya pada waktu yang tepat, ketika seluruh pemangku kepentingan sudah diinformasikan. Ke depan, kami terus memantau perkembangan kondisi ekonomi di seluruh wilayah bisnis kami dan mengambil tindakan yang diperlukan,\u201d beber John Gardiner, juru bicara Ford Eropa di Cologne, Jerman.<br \/>\n            Ford sudah merakit mobil di Inggris sejak 1911 dan penutupan pabrik terakhir yang pernah dilakukannya adalah pabrik Dagenham, 2002 silam. Pabrik itu tadinya memproduksi Fiesta dan memaksa pemutusan hubungan kerja 2.000 karyawan.<br \/><br \/>\nPertanyaan<br \/>\n1. Menurut Anda, bagaimana kelompok ekonomi deskriptif, kelompok teori ekonomi, dan kelompok ekonomi terapan membahas masalah di atas?<br \/>\n2.  Apakah masalah diatas termasuk masalah ekonomi mikro atau makro?<br \/>\n3. Menurut Anda, cabang ekonomi apa yang lebih tepat membahas masalah ekonomi dalam artikel di atas? Mengapa?<br \/><br \/>\n4. Adakah pada artikel di atas ditemukan pernyataan positif dan pernyataan normatif? Coba jelaskan.",

Ekonomi deskriptif<\/span> (descriptive economics)\n bekerja dengan mengumpulkan informasi-informasi faktual mengenai \nmasalah ekonomi. Ekonomi deskriptif menggambarkan keadaan perekonomian \nyang sebenarnya terjadi di masyarakat.<br \/><\/span><br \/><span><span>Teori Ekonomi <\/span>(economic theory) berusaha menggeneralisasikan data-data ekonomi dan memberikan penafsiran atas data tersebut.<br \/><br \/><\/span><br \/><span>Ekonomi Makro adalah bagian dari ilmu ekonomi yang khusus mempelajari mekanisme kerja perekonomian secara keseluruhan<br \/>\u00a0<br \/>No. 2.....ekonomi mikro<br \/><br \/>No. 3<br \/><br \/><\/span><br \/><span>1. Ilmu ekonomi moneter<br \/><span>\u00a0 \u00a0 Ilmu ekonomi moneter adalah cabang ilmu ekonomi yang membahas tentang uang, perbankan, dan lembaga keuangan lainny<br \/><\/span><\/span><br \/><span>2. Ilmu ekonomi publik<br \/><span>\u00a0 \u00a0 Ilmu ekonomi publik adalah cabang ilmu ekonomi yang membahas tentang kebijakan pemerintah dalam perekonomian.<br \/><br \/><\/span><\/span><br \/> Ilmu ekonomi industri<br \/><span>\u00a0 \u00a0 \nIlmu ekonomi industri adalah cabang ilmu ekonomi yang memfokuskan \npembahasan pada interaksi berbagai perusahaan dalam suatu industri<br \/><\/span><br \/><span><span>4. Ilmu ekonomi internasional\u00a0<\/span><br \/><span>\u00a0 \u00a0 \nIlmu ekonomi internasional adalah cabang ilmu ekonomi yang membahas \ntentang kegiatan perekonomian antarbangsa atau antarnegara<br \/><\/span><\/span><br \/><span>5. Ilmu ekonomi regional<br \/><span>\u00a0 \u00a0 \nIlmu ekonomi regional adalah cabang ilmu ekonomi yang antara lain \nmembahas tentang interaksi ekonomi antarwilayah dan proses perkembangan \nsuatu wilayah<br \/><br \/><\/span><\/span><br \/><span>6. CEO ford,alan mulally,mengatakan industri otomotif di eropa harus mengubah ukurannya sesuai kondisi pasar supaya bisa tetap untung.<br \/>Sepanjang 2011,produksi pabrik southampton hanya 230.000 unit pertahun.\"jadi sangat jelas kondisi ini jauhdari semestinya,\"jelas brian.<br \/>Stephen odell dijadwalkan bertemu dengan serikat pkerja dari sluruh pabrik di inggris di dunton,hari ini.\"Belum ada topik apa yang akan dibicarakn, \"jelas roger maddison,pemimpin serikat pkerja ford dri pabrik southampton.<br \/>\"Kami akan melakukan pengumuman selanjutnya pada waktu yang tepat,ketika sluruh pemangku kpentingan sudah diinformasikan. kedepan kami trus memantau prkmbangan kondisi ekonomi sluruh wilayah bisnis kami dan mngambil tindakan yg diperlukan,\"beber john gardier,juru bcara ford eropa di cologne,jerman.<br \/>Ford sudah merakit mobil di inggris sejak di inggris 1911 dan pnutupan pabrik terakhir yg prnh dilakukannya adalah pabrik degenham,2002 silam. pabrik itu tadinya\u00a0memproduksi fiesta dan memaksa pmutusan hubungan krja 2.000 karyawan.<br \/><br \/>PERTANYAAN :<br \/>1.Menurut pemahaman ilmu ekonomi siapa yang relatif tepat dengan artikel diatas\/coba jelaskan alasan anda?<br \/>2.Menurut anda bgaimana klompok deskriptif klompok teori ekonomi dan kelompok terapan membahas masalah di atas?<br \/>3.Menurut anda cabang ekonomi apa yg lbih tepat membahas masalh ekonomi dalam artikel di atas?mengapa?<br \/>adakah pada artikel di atas ditemukan prtanyaan normatif?coba jelaskan?<br \/><br \/><br \/>",

                        "content": "Pottery is one of the oldest and most widespread of the<br \/>\ndecorative arts, consisting chiefly of functional objects (such<br \/>\nas vessels, plates, and bowls) made of clay and hardened with<br \/>\nheat. Earthenware is the oldest and simplest form; stoneware<br \/>\nis fired at a high temperature to cause it to vitrify and harden;<br \/>\nand porcelain is a fine, generally translucent form of pottery.<br \/>\nPersian pottery (sometimes called Iranian pottery) refers to the<br \/>\npottery works made by the artists of Persia (Iran). The ceramic<br \/>\nart of Persia is one of the world's greatest and most influential<br \/>\nartistic traditions.<br \/>\nThe history goes back to early Neolithic Age (7th<br \/>\nmillennium BCE) with the production of coarse, unglazed<br \/>\nwares. In 717 CE, when the Arab empire was one of the<br \/>\nstrongest, Persian pottery was developed based on Roman,<br \/>\nGreek, Egyptian, and Central Asiatic ideas. During the 9th<br \/>\ncentury under the Abbasid government, cobalt blue and<br \/>\nother metallic oxides to produce blues and greens were<br \/>\nused. Colors such as manganese purple, tomato red, olive<br \/>\ngreen, yellow and brown were applied to the surface and<br \/>\nthen covered with a transparent glaze, creating a glossy and<br \/>\nsmooth finish. By the 12th century, Persian ceramic styles<br \/>\nwere well established and they set the standards for further<br \/>\ninnovations and conventions.<br \/>\nRecent excavations and archaeological research<br \/>\nrevealed that there were four major pottery-manufacturing<br \/>\nareas in the Iranian plateau. These included the western part<br \/>\nof the country, namely the area west of the Zagros mountains<br \/>\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (Gilan<br \/>\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as<br \/>\nfar as is known today, the earliest. The third region is located<br \/>\nin the northwestern part of the country, in Azarbaijan. The<br \/>\nfourth area is in the southeast, i.e. the Kerman region and<br \/>\nBaluchestan. To these four regions one may also add the<br \/>\nKavir area, where the history of pottery making can be dated<br \/>\nback to the 8th millennium BCE.<br \/>\nPersian pottery gained its renaissance, after its<br \/>\ndownfall due to Mongol conquest, during the Safavid period.<br \/>\nThe most important product in Kubachi ware of the Safavid<br \/>\nperiodis the polychromepainted. The designs appear in blue,<br \/>\nbrownish-red, yellow and green under clear glaze. Earthenware is the oldest and simplest form; stoneware\nis fired at a high temperature to cause it to vitrify and harden;\nand porcelain is a fine, generally translucent form of pottery.\nPersian pottery (sometimes called Iranian pottery) refers to the\npottery works made by the artists of Persia (Iran). The ceramic\nart of Persia is one of the world's greatest and most influential\nartistic traditions.\nThe history goes back to early Neolithic Age (7th\nmillennium BCE) with the production of coarse, unglazed\nwares. In 717 CE, when the Arab empire was one of the\nstrongest, Persian pottery was developed based on Roman,\nGreek, Egyptian, and Central Asiatic ideas. During the 9th\ncentury under the Abbasid government, cobalt blue and\nother metallic oxides to produce blues and greens were\nused. Colors such as manganese purple, tomato red, olive\ngreen, yellow and brown were applied to the surface and\nthen covered with a transparent glaze, creating a glossy and\nsmooth finish. By the 12th century, Persian ceramic styles\nwere well established and they set the standards for further\ninnovations and conventions.\nRecent excavations and archaeological research\nrevealed that there were four major pottery-manufacturing\nareas in the Iranian plateau. These included the western part\nof the country, namely the area west of the Zagros mountains\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (<em>Gila<\/em>n\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as\nfar as is known today, the earliest. The third region is located\nin the northwestern part of the country, in Azarbaijan. The\nfourth area is in the southeast, i.e. the Kerman region and\nBaluchestan. To these four regions one <em>may<\/em> also add the\nKavir area, where the history of pottery making can be dated\nback to the 8th millennium BCE.\nPersian pottery gained its renaissance, after its\ndownfall due to Mongol conquest, during the Safavid period.\nThe most important product in Kubachi ware of the Safavid\nperiodis the polychromepainted. The designs appear in blue,\nbrownish-red, yellow and green under clear glaze. Portraits of\npeople are painted against floral or simple scroll backgrounds.\nOthers depict landscapes or just flowers. Apart from large\ndishes, small bowls, dishes and jugs are also known in these\ntypes. By the 12th century, Persian ceramic styles<br \/>\nwere well established and they set the standards for further<br \/>\ninnovations and conventions.<br \/>\nRecent excavations and archaeological research<br \/>\nrevealed that there were four major pottery-manufacturing<br \/>\nareas in the Iranian plateau. These included the western part<br \/>\nof the country, namely the area west of the Zagros mountains<br \/>\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (Gilan<br \/>\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as<br \/>\nfar as is known today, the earliest. The third region is located<br \/>\nin the northwestern part of the country, in Azarbaijan. The<br \/>\nfourth area is in the southeast, i.e. the Kerman region and<br \/>\nBaluchestan. To these four regions one may also add the<br \/>\nKavir area, where the history of pottery making can be dated<br \/>\nback to the 8th millennium BCE.<br \/><br \/>\nPersian pottery gained its renaissance, after its<br \/>\ndownfall due to Mongol conquest, during the Safavid period.<br \/>\nThe most important product in Kubachi ware of the Safavid<br \/>\nperiodis the polychromepainted. The designs appear in blue,<br \/>\nbrownish-red, yellow and green under clear glaze. Portraits of<br \/>\npeople are painted against floral or simple scroll backgrounds.<br \/>\nOthers depict landscapes or just flowers. Apart from large<br \/>\ndishes, small bowls, dishes and jugs are also known in these<br \/>\ntypes. The beauty of Persian pottery during renaissance<br \/><br \/>\nperiod gained new impetus, and was partly under the<br \/>\ninfluence of Ottoman and European, and Chinese traditions.<br \/>\nIranian pottery also has white (gombroon) wares.<br \/>\nThe term \"Gombroon\" derives from the old name of modern<br \/>\nBander Abbas, which in Safavid times was an important<br \/>\nport on the Persian Gulf. The \"Gombroon\" ware has a hard<br \/>\nfaience body, which is considerably thinner than that of<br \/>\ncontemporary lustre ware. As often described, lustre ware<br \/>\nhas a very hard and compact white body and was decorated<br \/>\nin golden, brownish or reddish colour. Gombroon ware is<br \/>\noccasionally even translucent.<br \/>\nThrough the centuries, Persian potters have adopted<br \/>\nand refined newly introduced forms and blended them into<br \/>\ntheir own culture. (This article is adapted from three Internet sources:<br \/>\nhttp:\/\/www.merriam-webster.com\/dictionary\/pottery, http:\/\/en.wikipedia.<br \/>\norg\/wiki\/Persian_pottery,and http:\/\/www.cais-soas.com\/CAIS\/Art\/iranian<br \/>\n_pottery.htm)",

                        "highlighted_content": "Buat pertanyaan dan jawaban dalam bentuk bhs inggris dengan teks \"persian pottery\"\nPottery is one of the oldest and most widespread of the\ndecorative arts, consisting chiefly of functional objects (such\nas vessels, plates, and bowls) made of clay and hardened with\nheat. Earthenware is the oldest and simplest form; stoneware\nis fired at a high temperature to cause it to vitrify and harden;\nand porcelain is a fine, generally translucent form of pottery.\nPersian pottery (sometimes called Iranian pottery) refers to the\npottery works made by the artists of Persia (Iran). The ceramic\nart of Persia is one of the world's greatest and most influential\nartistic traditions.\nThe history goes back to early Neolithic Age (7th\nmillennium BCE) with the production of coarse, unglazed\nwares. In 717 CE, when the Arab empire was one of the\nstrongest, Persian pottery was developed based on Roman,\nGreek, Egyptian, and Central Asiatic ideas. During the 9th\ncentury under the Abbasid government, cobalt blue and\nother metallic oxides to produce blues and greens were\nused. Colors such as manganese purple, tomato red, olive\ngreen, yellow and brown were applied to the surface and\nthen covered with a transparent glaze, creating a glossy and\nsmooth finish. By the 12th century, Persian ceramic styles\nwere well established and they set the standards for further\ninnovations and conventions.\nRecent excavations and archaeological research\nrevealed that there were four major pottery-manufacturing\nareas in the Iranian plateau. These included the western part\nof the country, namely the area west of the Zagros mountains\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (<em>Gila<\/em>n\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as\nfar as is known today, the earliest. The third region is located\nin the northwestern part of the country, in Azarbaijan. The\nfourth area is in the southeast, i.e. the Kerman region and\nBaluchestan. To these four regions one <em>may<\/em> also add the\nKavir area, where the history of pottery making can be dated\nback to the 8th millennium BCE.\nPersian pottery gained its renaissance, after its\ndownfall due to Mongol conquest, during the Safavid period.\nThe most important product in Kubachi ware of the Safavid\nperiodis the polychromepainted. The designs appear in blue,\nbrownish-red, yellow and green under clear glaze. Portraits of\npeople are painted against floral or simple scroll backgrounds.\nOthers depict landscapes or just flowers. Apart from large\ndishes, small bowls, dishes and jugs are also known in these\ntypes. The beauty of Persian pottery during renaissance\nperiod gained new impetus, and was partly under the\ninfluence of Ottoman and European, and Chinese traditions.\nIranian pottery also has white (gombroon) wares.\nThe term \"Gombroon\" derives from the old name of modern\nBander Abbas, which in Safavid times was an important\nport on the Persian Gulf. The \"Gombroon\" ware has a hard\nfaience body, which is considerably thinner than that of\ncontemporary lustre ware. As often described, lustre ware\nhas a very hard and compact white body and was decorated\nin golden, brownish or reddish colour. Gombroon ware is\noccasionally even translucent.\nThrough the centuries, Persian potters have adopted\nand refined newly introduced forms and blended them into\ntheir own culture. (This article is adapted from three Internet sources:\nhttp:\/\/www.merriam-webster.com\/dictionary\/pottery, http:\/\/en.wikipedia.\norg\/wiki\/Persian_pottery,and http:\/\/www.cais-soas.com\/CAIS\/Art\/iranian\n_pottery.htm)",

                        "highlighted_content": "Buat pertanyaan dan jawaban dalam bentuk bhs inggris (10 soal) dengan teks \"persian pottery\"\nPottery is one of the oldest and most widespread of the\ndecorative arts, consisting chiefly of functional objects (such\nas vessels, plates, and bowls) made of clay and hardened with\nheat. Earthenware is the oldest and simplest form; stoneware\nis fired at a high temperature to cause it to vitrify and harden;\nand porcelain is a fine, generally translucent form of pottery.\nPersian pottery (sometimes called Iranian pottery) refers to the\npottery works made by the artists of Persia (Iran). The ceramic\nart of Persia is one of the world's greatest and most influential\nartistic traditions.\nThe history goes back to early Neolithic Age (7th\nmillennium BCE) with the production of coarse, unglazed\nwares. In 717 CE, when the Arab empire was one of the\nstrongest, Persian pottery was developed based on Roman,\nGreek, Egyptian, and Central Asiatic ideas. During the 9th\ncentury under the Abbasid government, cobalt blue and\nother metallic oxides to produce blues and greens were\nused. Colors such as manganese purple, tomato red, olive\ngreen, yellow and brown were applied to the surface and\nthen covered with a transparent glaze, creating a glossy and\nsmooth finish. By the 12th century, Persian ceramic styles\nwere well established and they set the standards for further\ninnovations and conventions.\nRecent excavations and archaeological research\nrevealed that there were four major pottery-manufacturing\nareas in the Iranian plateau. These included the western part\nof the country, namely the area west of the Zagros mountains\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (<em>Gila<\/em>n\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as\nfar as is known today, the earliest. The third region is located\nin the northwestern part of the country, in Azarbaijan. The\nfourth area is in the southeast, i.e. the Kerman region and\nBaluchestan. To these four regions one <em>may<\/em> also add the\nKavir area, where the history of pottery making can be dated\nback to the 8th millennium BCE.\nPersian pottery gained its renaissance, after its\ndownfall due to Mongol conquest, during the Safavid period.\nThe most important product in Kubachi ware of the Safavid\nperiodis the polychromepainted. The designs appear in blue,\nbrownish-red, yellow and green under clear glaze. Portraits of\npeople are painted against floral or simple scroll backgrounds.\nOthers depict landscapes or just flowers. Apart from large\ndishes, small bowls, dishes and jugs are also known in these\ntypes. The beauty of Persian pottery during renaissance\nperiod gained new impetus, and was partly under the\ninfluence of Ottoman and European, and Chinese traditions.\nIranian pottery also has white (gombroon) wares.\nThe term \"Gombroon\" derives from the old name of modern\nBander Abbas, which in Safavid times was an important\nport on the Persian Gulf. The \"Gombroon\" ware has a hard\nfaience body, which is considerably thinner than that of\ncontemporary lustre ware. As often described, lustre ware\nhas a very hard and compact white body and was decorated\nin golden, brownish or reddish colour. Gombroon ware is\noccasionally even translucent.\nThrough the centuries, Persian potters have adopted\nand refined newly introduced forms and blended them into\ntheir own culture. (This article is adapted from three Internet sources:\nhttp:\/\/www.merriam-webster.com\/dictionary\/pottery, http:\/\/en.wikipedia.\norg\/wiki\/Persian_pottery,and http:\/\/www.cais-soas.com\/CAIS\/Art\/iranian\n_pottery.htm)",
                        "snippet_content": "Zagros mountains\n(Lurestan), and the area south of the Caspian Sea (<em>Gila<\/em>n\nand Mazandaran). These two areas are chronologically as\nfar as"

                        "content": "Harapan untuk Mas Galang<br \/>\nArini Izzataddini<br \/><br \/><br \/>\n\u201cZita, ayo tidur sayaang. Sudah jam setengah sepuluh niih. Memangnya besok kamu tidak sekolah ? Ayo cepat tidur Zita\u201d Mama menyuruhku tidur sambil berlalu ke kamarnya. \u201c Iya maa.\u201d Ujarku yang sedang menonton sinetron kesukaanku. Aku matikan tivi dan naik tangga menuju kamarku.<br \/>\nAku langsung naik ke kasurku untuk tidur. Karena aku sudah mulai mengantuk. Tapii. Kok aku nggak bisa tidur ya ? Seperti ada yang kurang. Oh iya ! Aku lupa menulis diary. Kebiasaanku setiap sebelum tidur adalah menulis diary. Tapi kenapa sekarang aku lupa ya ?<br \/>\nAku langsung mengambil diaryku di lemari dan mulai menulisnya.<br \/><br \/>\nDear Diary,<br \/>\nHari ini, aku punya satu cerita yang mengaharukan tentang sepupuku sendiri.. Mas Galang namanya.<br \/>\nPada tahun 1995, lahir 5 orang anak dari lima pasang suami istri. Ibu-ibu yang melahirkan berasal dari satu keluarga besar yang sama. Kakek dan Nenek sangat bahagia. Mereka langsung memiliki 5 cucu sekaligus di tahun itu. Galang, Dimaz, Agung, Rania dan aku. Mereka lahir normal dan sehat. Itu terjadi lima belas tahun yang lalu..<br \/>\nDi tahun ajaran ini, kami berlima seharusnya akan menjalani UAS-BN. Empat anak diantara kami telah bersiap-siap untuk melakukannya. Tapi satu anak lagi? Ia hanya bisa di rumah melakukan kegiatan yang tak menentu\u2026<br \/>\nYa, mas Galang namanya. Putra ketiga dari kakak ayahku yang tertua. Dia menderita autis. Mamaku masih suka bercerita bahwa pada tahun pertama, mas Galang terlihat sebagai anak yang paling sehat diantara kami. Tinggi besar, tampan, dan sangat aktif. Tapi makin lama, makin terlihat bahwa dia tidak memiliki kemampuan berkomunikasi dan bersosialisasi yang baik.<br \/>\nSaat ini, kondisinya sangat mengkhawatirkan. Karena masih belum dapat berkomunikasi dengan baik. Bahkan belum dapat melakukan pekerjaan-pekerjaan yang menunjukkan kemandiriannya. Jadi selama ini bude dan Pakdeku sangat memproteksi dirinya. Memang kasihan mas Galang, orang tuanya bukan orang yang berpunya. Bahkan\u2026.rumahnya di pinggir sekaligus di atas sungai. Rumah yang sungguh membahayakan untuk kondisi mas Galang yang seperti ini. Aku ingin menangis jika aku berkunjung ke rumahnya. Wilayahnya tidak layak dan rumahnya bukan seperti rumah melainkan gudang kecil.<br \/>\nUsaha-usaha orangtuanya sedikit membuahkan hasil. Ayahnya belum punya pekerjaan tetap. Hanya seorang perangkai dan penjual bunga yang tak selalu mendapat order untuk dikerjakan. Kakaknya masih kelas 11 sekarang. Mas Galang punya satu kakak lagi, yang sedang bekerja di Filipina. Dan ia satu-satunya tulang punggung di keluarga itu. Selain keadaan mas Galang yang mengkhawatirkan, ibunya lebih mengkhawatirkan. Bude Lina, jika kupanggil dirinya, terkena Thalasemia hingga saat ini. Uang mereka tak cukup untuk menyembuhkan Bude Lina dan melaksanakan terapi autis mas Galang sekaligus.<br \/>\nAnaknya tampan dan selalu ingin tahu. Kini, ia sudah mulai dapat sedikit berbicara walaupun belum mampu berfikir jelas. Mas Galang sudah tumbuh lebih tinggi dari aku, Dimaz, Agung,dan Rania. Tapi walaupun begitu, keadaan non fisiknya jauh tertinggal dari kami. Tidak pernah ada yang menduga, karena Mas Galang terlahir normal dan sama seperti kami semua.<br \/>\nPapaku bilang, dulu keluarga nenek tidak mampu. Sebagai kakak pertama, Bude Lina menjadi tulang punggung keluarga. Ia tak sekolah hingga S1. Langsung saja bekerja. Jadi, beliau sekolahkan adik-adiknya. Memang, seluruh keluarga besar kami saat ini telah turut membantu ekonomi keluarga bude, namun karena masing-masing memiliki tanggungan keluarga yang juga tidak sedikit, maka bantuan bagi mas Galang masihlah jauh dari kebutuhan. Menghidupi keluarga sehari-hari, membantu pengobatan mas Galang, dan bude Lina sekaligus.<br \/>\nHarapanku, mas Galang dapat sembuh dan dapat bermain dan belajar bersama kami, atau paling tidak, dia mampu membantu dirinya sendiri, sehinga dapat menjadi manusia yang mandiri, dan kelak tidak bergantung pada orang lain. Aku ingin sekali mas Galang dapat menjalani terapi yang Intensif, agar kondisi itu dapat terwujud. Dan aku ingin bude Lina berkurang beban hidupnya, sebagaimana yang selalu beliau rasakan selama ini\u2026.. Ini adalah Harapanku.<br \/>\n****<br \/>\n\u201cHoaam.                         "content": "Text\u00a0 1 is for questions number 1-3.<br \/><br \/>\nIcebergs are mountains of freshwater ice floating in the ocean. They are huge chunks broken off from the great masses of land ice called glaciers.<br \/>\nAlmost all of Greenland and Antarctica are covered by glaciers the year round. Glaciers also cover parts of Alaska. They are formed by layers of packed snow. Glacier may be thousands of meters thick. Their front ends, or tongues, reach down to the sea. At the coast the tips of the tongues break off, plunge into the oceans, and become icebergs. This process is called calving.<br \/>\nWhen calving occurs, a loud cracking noise fills the air. Sometimes a low rumbling can be heard for hours before the ice actually breaks away. People close enough can hear the hissing of air as it escapes from bubbles bursting in the ice along the break.<br \/>\nGlaciers calve all year round. Just as many icebergs break off in winter as in summer. But in winter their passageway to open the sea is often jammed with masses of frozen seawater. Icebergs pile up behind this jam of sea ice. In the spring, when the ice block is broken, a whole fleet of icebergs may sail out toward the open ocean.<br \/>\nIcebergs from the eastern coast of Greenland drift southward. They are carried by the Greenland Current, which then swings them northward around the tip of the island. Part of the way up the coast the icebergs are caught in the cold Labrador Current and carried southward toward Newfound-land<br \/>\nOn the way, most of the icebergs become grounded among the many islands and bays along the Labrador coast. The others float on toward the open sea. Off Newfoundland they are caught by a warm current from the south called the Gulf Stream. Icebergs that do not ground and remain in the Labrador Current often enter the lanes used by ships crossing the Atlantic Ocean.<br \/>\nAn iceberg starts to break up almost as soon as it is afloat. Cracks appear and become filled with water from ice that melts during the day. When this melted water freezes at night, it expands and widens the cracks. The ice is weakened, and pieces of iceberg break off and float away. The iceberg becomes smaller and smaller. Most icebergs melt completely within a few days of entering the Gulf Stream.<br \/><br \/>\n1. What does the text tell us about? <br \/>\n2. When and why do the the fleet of icebergs sail out toward the open ocean?<br \/>\n3. What is the purposes of the text  and explain the generic structure of the above text? <br \/>",

                        "content": "Tolong dong cek ,apakah report text ini sudah benar?kalo belum tolong ditambahkan dan kalo salah tolong dikoreksi.<br \/><br \/>\nLizard <br \/>\nLizard is the animals that belong to reptile that has scales and four legs. Based on the size of the body, these animals are classified into two groups that are small-bodied lizards like home lizards, sand lizards, geckos, and big-bodied lizard such as Biawak, and Komodo.  This animal belongs to cold-bodied animals. They need sun to regulate their body temperature.<br \/><br \/>\nLarge-bodied lizard\u2019s length can reach more than 3 m. Lizard\u2019 body is generally filled by scales but some are smooth and shiny like type of Infra ordo Scincomorpha. Lizard has various habitats to live. Most of lizards live on the land (terrestrial), some of them lives inside soil or sand (tonsorial) while some snake hangs around on the top or in the trunk of the tree (arboreal).
